Otherwise set it to false.\n    </p>\n   </td>\n  </tr>\n  <tr>\n   <td>\n    delayInterval\n   </td>\n   <td>\n    <p>\n     Set the timestamp of the time until when the SLA must be marked as excluded.\n\t\t\tIgnore this field if \"excludeSLA\" is marked as false.\n    </p>\n   </td>\n  </tr>\n  <tr>\n   <td>\n    slaDescription\n   </td>\n   <td>\n    <p>\n     Description of the SLA. ## Update Plan SLA




This operation updates the SLA (service level agreement) for a plan.

[_More Details_](http://documentation.commvault.com/commvault/v11/article?p=features/rest_api/operations/put_plan_sla.htm)
<h2>
 Request Body
</h2>
<table width="331">
 
  <tr>
   <td>
    Name
   </td>
   <td>
    Description
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    level
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Set if the plan must use its own SLA or the Commcell's SLA.
    </p>
    
    <p>
     Permitted values -
     
     "SYSTEM_DEFAULT_SLA" - If the SLA must be set to the Commcell's default  SLA
     
     "SLA_FOR_LAST_N_DAYS" - If you want to define a custom SLA period for the plan
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    slaDays
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     The number of days (type must be int) for the SLA period. Ignore this attribute if the level is "SYSTEM_DEFAULT_SLA"
     
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    excludeSLA
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Set to true if the plan's SLA must be marked as excluded. Otherwise set it to false.
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    delayInterval
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Set the timestamp of the time until when the SLA must be marked as excluded.
			Ignore this field if "excludeSLA" is marked as false.
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    slaDescription
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Description of the SLA. This is an optional attribute.
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    entityType
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Always set it as "PLAN_ENTITY"
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
  <tr>
   <td>
    inheritedSLA
   </td>
   <td>
    <p>
     Always set it as mentioned in the sample
    </p>
   </td>
  </tr>
 
</table>
